convertVSSheetForWPUpload

This script will prepare our VitalSignsXl Doc for upload.

  1. It uses the meta data table to replace the datasheets column headers with a shortname
  2. Then empties columns that should not have their data uploaded yet according to section
  3. Then it Deletes placeholder columns for our wishlist indicators
xlsheet = '19' year = '20'import pandas as pd # df = pd.read_excel(open('VS19_Indicator_Data_Form.xlsm', 'rb'), sheet_name="Vital Signs 19 Indicators", header=None, names=['vsid', 'xlsmid', 'longname','shortname', 'UPLOAD_WP',]) df = pd.read_excel(open('VS'+xlsheet+'_Indicator_Data_Form.xlsm', 'rb'), sheet_name="Vital Signs "+xlsheet+" Indicators") df = df[['ShortName', 'Section']] df.ShortName = df.ShortName.astype(str).str[:-2] df.loc[-1] = ['CSA2010', 'Section'] df.index = df.index + 1 df.sort_index(inplace=True) display( df.head(1) )
ShortName Section
0 CSA2010 Section

Now Remove Data from Columns Not on Our Publishing List.

keep = ['Section', 'Crime and Safety','Census Demographics', 'Workforce and Economic Development', 'Sustainability', 'Housing and Community Development', 'Children and Family Health', 'Arts and Culture', 'Education and Youth'] rm = [] # For Each Column for currentColumn in vsdf.columns: # Get the Section indSection = df[ df['ShortName'] == currentColumn ]['Section'].values[0] # Delete Records if Not In Keep List if ( not indSection in set( keep ) ): vsdf[currentColumn] = '' # Delete columns if on wishlist. vsdf = vsdf[ df[ df['ShortName'] != 'n' ].ShortName.values ] vsdf = vsdf.add_suffix(year) vsdf.rename(columns = {f"CSA2010{year}": "CSA2010"}, inplace=True) vsdf.head()

In Maryland, all students who entered 9th grade in or after 2005 are required to take and pass the High School Assessments (H.S.A.) in order to graduate, including students in special education, English language learners (ELLs), and students with 504 plans. There are currently three H.S.A. exams: English, Algebra/Data Analysis; and Biology (a H.S.A. in Government has since been discontinued). Students can retake the HSAs as many times as necessary to pass., Years: 2009-2010, 2010-2011, 2011-2012, 2012-2013, 2013-2014}}, {Indicator: {IndicatorName: Percentage of Students Passing H.S.A.
